	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: oidplus.min.js.php');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('oidplus.min.js.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): oidplus.min.js.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') != 'ac4c33c37a64d3ab60c279212867e5473230b9c4') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.js.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('oidplus.min.js.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of oidplus.min.js.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') !== 'ac4c33c37a64d3ab60c279212867e5473230b9c4') {
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') !== '2fbe5378c3da614c3449e37a41bc5dd440b96ee4') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: oidplus.min.js.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('oidplus.min.js.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('oidplus.min.js.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('oidplus.min.js.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('oidplus.min.js.php') !== 'ac4c33c37a64d3ab60c279212867e5473230b9c4') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): oidplus.min.js.php');

if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css') != 'bb8db9fac366f95817c6e3828f323d6616454a10') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css') !== 'bb8db9fac366f95817c6e3828f323d6616454a10') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css') !== '8316aaddf2463a60ce0dc994ce5dd30878b65962') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css') !== 'bb8db9fac366f95817c6e3828f323d6616454a10') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/design/default/oidplus_base.css');
		}
	}
}

	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
	writefile_3();
	if (!is_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css') != '6166ce1b26ae01af88235cca071d7300bb87fa7d') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css') !== '6166ce1b26ae01af88235cca071d7300bb87fa7d') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css') !== '11ce58e82e4d8f9aba9e04b93810d4728a8d0bf7') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_3();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css') !== '6166ce1b26ae01af88235cca071d7300bb87fa7d') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/design/ironbase/oidplus_base.css');
		}
	}
}

		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if (sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') != '097850b38dc78359c9a97e7d1725f2629865544c') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '097850b38dc78359c9a97e7d1725f2629865544c') {
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '13d8f5a7c2207e0af25c4a9fc8723ed8049192d4') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$tmp = pathinfo('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml') !== '097850b38dc78359c9a97e7d1725f2629865544c') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): plugins/viathinksoft/language/dede/messages.xml');
